# Comments for Question 4, LLM=Gemma 3 27B

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=7.9)
    The story effectively uses the Napoleonic bee pin as a symbol that evolves from representing "ambition and fragility" to embodying resilience and rebuilding. The central theme of finding beauty in broken places and reimagining painful endings resonates emotionally. The narrative skillfully shifts from literal design work to metaphorical reconstruction of the self. While the story shows rather than tells emotional development, some metaphors ("pressure cooker of unspoken grief") feel slightly overwrought.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=8.7)
    The story achieves remarkable thematic depth through its exploration of sensitivity as both burden and gift. The metaphor of knots as trapped memories works brilliantly, and the subtext about embracing rather than escaping one's limitations resonates emotionally. The ending delivers a philosophical payoff that elevates the entire narrative. The writing shows restraint and precision, with effective "showing" through concrete details rather than telling. The central conflict between isolation and connection is elegantly resolved.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=6.4)
    The story effectively uses the lamp as a symbol for fragmented consciousness and hope, creating emotional resonance in Tiber's transformation. However, the conflict lacks sufficient stakes or tension, and the theme of redemption through remembrance, while present, isn't explored with enough depth or nuance to elevate the piece beyond its surface narrative.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=8.5)

The writing employs effective symbolism, particularly in the pressed pennies as anchors to reality and the oscillating moon paths reflecting Tiber's internal journey. The ending delivers a subtle but meaningful shift in perspective that resonates beyond the immediate narrative.
